<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/heil#German" title="heil">heil</a></i>.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">heil</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/heils#English" title="heils">heils</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/heiling#English" title="heiling">heiling</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/heiled#English" title="heiled">heiled</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To greet with a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Sieg_Heil#English" title="Sieg Heil">Sieg Heil</a></span>.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="German">German</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: German">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/heile#German" title="heile">heile</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">chiefly colloquial; rarely in writing</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href="/wiki/heil#Middle_High_German" title="heil">heil</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/heil#Old_High_German" title="heil">heil</a></i>, from  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailaz">*hailaz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/k%C3%B3h%E2%82%82ilos&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/kóh₂ilos (page does not exist)">*kóh₂ilos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">healthy, whole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In older High German only used of the human body and soul; the modern use also of things is based on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href="/wiki/hel#Middle_Low_German" title="hel">hêl</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href="/wiki/hel#Old_Saxon" title="hel">hēl</a></i>. The more general sense “whole, entire” did not establish itself in standard German (except in fixed combinations like <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/heilfroh#German" title="heilfroh">heilfroh</a></i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/heel#Dutch" title="heel">heel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/heel#Low_German" title="heel">heel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/heil#Low_German" title="heil">heil</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/whole#English" title="whole">whole</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hale#English" title="hale">hale</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/hel#Danish" title="hel">hel</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:German_pronunciation" title="Appendix:German pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/haɪ̯l/</span></li>

<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:German/a%C9%AA%CC%AFl" title="Rhymes:German/aɪ̯l"><span class="IPA">-aɪ̯l</span></a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de">heil</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparative" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/heiler#German" title="heiler">heiler</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#superlative" title="Appendix:Glossary">superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am <a href="/wiki/heilsten#German" title="heilsten">heilsten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/whole" title="whole">whole</a>; <a href="/wiki/intact" title="intact">intact</a>; <a href="/wiki/unhurt" title="unhurt">unhurt</a>; <a href="/wiki/safe" title="safe">safe</a>
<dl><dd><i>Gut, dass du <b>heil</b> wieder zurück bist.</i> — “I’m glad you’re back <b>safe</b>.”</dd>
<dd><i>Die Tasse ist noch <b>heil</b>.</i> — “The cup is still <b>whole</b>.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in combination with certain nouns</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/sheltered" title="sheltered">sheltered</a>; <a href="/wiki/innocent" title="innocent">innocent</a>; <a href="/wiki/ideal" title="ideal">ideal</a>
<dl><dd><i><b>heile</b> Kindheit</i> — <b>innocent</b> childhood</dd>
<dd><i><b>heile</b> Welt</i> — <b>ideal</b> world</dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Norwegian_Nynorsk">Norwegian Nynorsk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Norwegian Nynorsk">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/heill#Old_Norse" title="heill">heill</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailaz">*hailaz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/k%C3%B3h%E2%82%82ilus&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/kóh₂ilus (page does not exist)">*kóh₂ilus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">healthy, whole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/whole#English" title="whole">whole</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_Nynorsk_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Norwegian Nynorsk phonology">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/hæɪl/</span> <small>(<a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:ANO#Pronunciation" class="mw-redirect" title="Wiktionary:ANO">example</a> of pronunciation)</small></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_4">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nn">heil</strong> (<i>masculine and feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><strong class="selflink">heil</strong></b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/heilt#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="heilt">heilt</a></b>, <i>definite singular and plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/heile#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="heile">heile</a></b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=heilare&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="heilare (page does not exist)">heilare</a></b>, <i>indefinite superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/wiki/heilast#Norwegian_Nynorsk" title="heilast">heilast</a></b>, <i>definite superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=heilaste&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="heilaste (page does not exist)">heilaste</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/whole" title="whole">whole</a>, not in <a href="/wiki/piece" title="piece">pieces</a></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_High_German">Old High German</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Old High German">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailaz">*hailaz</a></i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href="/wiki/hel#Old_Saxon" title="hel">hēl</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/hal#Old_English" title="hal">hāl</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/heill#Old_Norse" title="heill">heill</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got"><a href="/wiki/%F0%90%8C%B7%F0%90%8C%B0%F0%90%8C%B9%F0%90%8C%BB%F0%90%8D%83#Gothic" title="𐌷𐌰𐌹𐌻𐍃">𐌷𐌰𐌹𐌻𐍃</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href="/wiki/hails#Gothic" title="hails">hails</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vandalic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Vandalic language">Vandalic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="xvn"><a href="/wiki/eils#Vandalic" title="eils">eils</a></i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/k%C3%B3h%E2%82%82ilus&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/kóh₂ilus (page does not exist)">*kóh₂ilus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">healthy, whole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_5">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=heil&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hail%C4%85&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/hailą (page does not exist)">*hailą</a></i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/h%C3%A6l#Old_English" title="hæl">hæl</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/heill#Old_Norse" title="heill">heill</a></i>.
